				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dlc = "Arms Against Tyranny"
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = available_mio_tt
					show_mio_tooltip = ITA_vickers_terni_organization
					mio:ITA_vickers_terni_organization = {
						add_mio_size = 2
					}
				}
				else = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = available_designer
					show_ideas_tooltip = vickers_terni
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
					}
					add_tech_bonus = {
						bonus = 0.75
						uses = 1
						category = ship_modules_tech
						name = italian_focus
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_tech_bonus = {
						bonus = 0.75
						uses = 1
						category = naval_equipment
						name = italian_focus
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = empty_space_tt
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				ITA_army_org_regain = 0.05
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_army_reform_tt2
			add_tech_bonus = {
				bonus = 0.35
				uses = 1
				category = industry
				name = italian_focus
			}
		}
		search_filters = {
			FOCUS_FILTER_HISTORICAL
			FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_REFORM
			FOCUS_FILTER_RESEARCH
			FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

		id = ITA_mechanization

			}

			unlock_decision_tooltip = ITA_fund_armoured_car_research

				add_tech_bonus = {
					category = cat_armored_cars
					name = ITA_fund_armoured_car_research
					bonus = 1

		}

			FOCUS_FILTER_HISTORICAL
			FOCUS_FILTER_RESEARCH
			FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_REFORM
		}
	}
	focus = {
